***alderman.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:alderman.html>alderman</a> (119865)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:alderman.html>alderman</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">aldermon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">ealdorman</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">ealdormann</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href = vnd.unilang:ealdor.html>ealdor</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">elder, parent, chief, prince, author</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">mann</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">ealdorman</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:alderman.html>alderman</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">aldermen</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A member of a municipal legislative body in a city or town.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> historical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete  <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A half-crown coin; its value, 30 pence.
<ul><li><b>1859</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/J.C._Hotten" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:J.C. Hotten">J.C. Hotten</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/A_Dictionary_of_Modern_Slang,_Cant,_and_Vulgar_Words" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:A Dictionary of Modern Slang, Cant, and Vulgar Words">A Dictionary of Modern <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>Slang</a>, Cant, and Vulgar <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>Words</a></a></i>
<dl><dd><i>Half-a-crown</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> known as an <span style="font-variant:small-caps;"><a class="mw-selflink selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:alderman.html>alderman</a></a></span>, <span style="font-variant:small-caps;"><a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a> a bull</span>, <span style="font-variant:small-caps;"><a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a> a tusheroon</span>, and a <span style="font-variant:small-caps;">madza caroon</span>; whilst a <i>crown</i> piece, or <i>five <a href = vnd.unilang:shillings.html>shillings</a></i>, may be called either a <span style="font-variant:small-caps;">bull</span>, or a <span style="font-variant:small-caps;">caroon</span>, or a <span style="font-variant:small-caps;">cartwheel</span>, or a <span style="font-variant:small-caps;">coachwheel</span>, or a <span style="font-variant:small-caps;">thick-un</span>, or a <span style="font-variant:small-caps;">tusheroon</span>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">baillie</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Scotland</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ul>
</body>

<ol><li>thus, so</li>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijwoord.html>Bijwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***alf.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:alf.html>alf</a> (7335)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:alf.html>alf</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:alf.html>alf</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*albiz</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*albʰós</i>. Doublet with Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:elf.html>elf</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:elf.html>elf</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a modern borrowing from English.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:alf.html>alf</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:alf.html>alven</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:alf.html>alfje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">alve</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>a type of folkloristic humanoid or spirit; an <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:elf.html>elf</a></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***alfa.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:alfa.html>alfa</a> (9794)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἄλφα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">álpha</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Semitic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Semitic languages">Semitic</a></span> origin.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:algoritme.html>algoritme</a> (21424)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">algorithmus</i>, a by-form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">algorismus</i> introduced under the influence of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἀριθμός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">arithmós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">number</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. A Latinization of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">الْخُوَارِزْمِيّ</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">al-ḵuwārizmiyy</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">native of Khowarizm</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, surname of the Persian mathematician <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Muhammad_ibn_M%C5%ABs%C4%81_al-Khw%C4%81rizm%C4%AB" class="extiw" title="w:Muhammad ibn Mūsā al-Khwārizmī">Muhammad ibn Mūsā Al-Khwārizmī</a>.

***allemaal.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:allemaal.html>allemaal</a> (156)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">altemaal</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">altemȃle</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">all at once; altogether</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:helemaal.html>helemaal</a></i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">allemal</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:allemaal.html>allemaal</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">all</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">everyone</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:allemaal.html>allemaal</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a>'re doing it <b>all</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:allemaal.html>allemaal</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a>'re <b>all</b> doing it.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Despite its status as a pronoun, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:allemaal.html>allemaal</a></i> can not serve as a subject in a sentence <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> in such <a href = vnd.unilang:cases.html>cases</a> it complements another pronoun. It can, however, serve as an object.
</p>
<hr><h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synoniemen"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:synoniemen.html>Synoniemen</a></i></span></h5>
<ul><li><a href = vnd.unilang:alles.html>alles</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:allen.html>allen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:alle.html>alle</a></li></ul>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
</body> 
***allemachtig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:allemachtig.html>allemachtig</a> (3449)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:almachtig.html>almachtig</a></i> with shwa insertion.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:allemachtig.html>allemachtig</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">An expression of surprise or excitement:</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:oh.html>oh</a> my <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a>!, holy <a href = vnd.unilang:macaroni.html>macaroni</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a> Almighty!

<dl><dd><b><a href = vnd.unilang:oh.html>Oh</a> my!</b> Eighty-eight powerful <a href = vnd.unilang:trucks.html>trucks</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brought.html>brought</a> beautiful, soft furs.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

***allochtoon.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:allochtoon.html>allochtoon</a> (109758)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:allochtone.html>allochtone</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἄλλος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">állos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">other</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">χθών</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">khthṓn</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">earth, ground</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:allochtoon.html>allochtoon</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:allochtoon.html>allochtoner</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">allochtoonst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>allochthonous</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:allochtoon.html>allochtoon</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:allochtonen.html>allochtonen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:allochtoon.html>allochtoontje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A person (or thing) originating abroad.
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law<span class="ib-comma">,</span> demography</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A person of non-native descent, having <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> born abroad or having foreign parents or grandparents <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">legal and demographic definitions vary</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>.</li></ol></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> potentially  offensive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A person of Non-Western descent.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Use in the meaning “person of Non-Western descent” <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> often considered <a href = vnd.unilang:racist.html>racist</a> and considered incorrect by those adhering to more formal definitions. The word in reference to people <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> avoided by the Dutch government in the formal senses as well since 2016.
</p>

***allooi.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:allooi.html>allooi</a> (71218)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aloy</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">aloi</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:allooi.html>allooi</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:allooi.html>allooien</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>quality, level, type, <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a>

***almaar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:almaar.html>almaar</a> (29470)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">all</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">but</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:almaar.html>almaar</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>all the time
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:almaar.html>almaar</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werk.html>werk</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>He <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> always working.</dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:situatie.html>situatie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:almaar.html>almaar</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:erger.html>erger</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>The situation keeps getting worse.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The variant <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:alsmaar.html>alsmaar</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> widely used in <a href = vnd.unilang:spoken.html>spoken</a> language, but not accepted by everyone, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> therefore advised to write <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:almaar.html>almaar</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijwoord.html>Bijwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:almaar.html>almaar</a></b>

***alras.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:alras.html>alras</a> (109755)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ras.html>ras</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">quick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:alras.html>alras</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>quickly, soon</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijwoord.html>Bijwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> (27)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">alse</i>, an unstressed form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">also</i> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:alzo.html>alzo</a></i>).

<li>when, as soon as

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:alsem.html>alsem</a> (61843)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">alsene</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:alsem.html>alsem</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:alsem.html>alsems</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> artemisia, any herb of the genus <i>Artemisia</i>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> the <a href = vnd.unilang:buds.html>buds</a> and flowers of the artemisia plants, used as a herb</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:alsem.html>alsem</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:plantkunde.html>plantkunde</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:alle.html>alle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:planten.html>planten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> composietengeslacht <a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Artemisia" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Artemisia"><span style="color:green;"><i>Artemisia</i></span></a> <img alt="op Wikispecies" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/14px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png" decoding="async" width="14" height="18" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/21px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/28px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png 2x" data-file-width="125" data-file-height="160" />, w.<a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a>. bijvoet, averuit, absint-alsem</li></ol>

***alsjeblieft.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:alsjeblieft.html>alsjeblieft</a> (233)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jou.html>jou</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:belieft.html>belieft</a></i>.
